â”‚                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚ ### netNTLMv2 Hash Format for `john` and `hashcat`                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚ The netNTLMv2 hash format typically follows this structure:                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚ ```                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚ <username>::<domain>:<challenge>:<response>:<target information>                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚ ```                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚ - **username**: The username of the account (e.g., robb.stark).                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚ - **domain**: The domain name (e.g., NORTH).                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚ - **challenge**: A 16-byte challenge from the server.                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚ - **response**: The 24-byte response from the client.                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚ - **target information**: Additional information that might be included, but is not always necessary for cracking.                                        â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚ ### Example                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚ For `john` and `hashcat`, the hash might look like this:                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚ ```                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚ robb.stark::NORTH:1122334455667788:abcdefabcdefabcdefabcdefabcdefabcdef:0101000000000000...                                                               â”‚
â”‚ ```                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚ ### Steps to Revise Captured Hashes                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚ 1. **Ensure Proper Delimiters**: Use colons (`:`) to separate each component.                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ 2. **Verify Each Component**: Make sure the username, domain, challenge, and response are correctly captured and formatted.                               â”‚
â”‚ 3. **Check for Additional Information**: Some tools might require additional target information, but this is not always necessary.                        â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚ ### Key Findings                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚ - The netNTLMv2 hash format is crucial for successful loading into `john` and `hashcat`.                                                                  â”‚
â”‚ - Proper structuring of the hash with correct delimiters and components is necessary.                                                                     â”‚
â”‚ - The domain name, username, challenge, and response must be accurately captured and formatted.                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚ By ensuring the captured hashes for NORTH\robb.stark and NORTH\eddard.stark are revised according to this format, you can proceed with offline cracking   â”‚
â”‚ or pass-the-hash attacks using `john` or `hashcat`.                                                                                                       â”‚
